Comment: tardis.kiss said "♢
☆ I used: 8B Derwent Graphic 12 Pencils, Prismacolour Coloured Pencils, Prismacolour silver & gold metallic pens, and a Gelly Roll gel pen☆
.
☆Trades, requests, collaborations, and commissions are closed☆
.
My grandmother asked me to draw this for her friend as an Easter gift.
I'm pretty happy with the way this turned out! It took about 3-4 hours, but it was worth it.
Aghh I really wish I could keep this because I'm very proud of how it turned out, but I'm hoping that my grandma's friend will enjoy it just as much. Hopefully she'll like it!
//
#easter #easterbunny #art #bunny #happyeaster #myart"

Comment: themusicroomatmidway said "Super excited to be playing "The Amazing Note Race" with third grade today!! We have been learning about the note names on the treble staff, and today we are reviewing by playing this awesome game. The kids will be in two teams. While the music plays, they will pass the tater tot. When the music stops, I'll display a note on the board. The person who has the tot must run and put the tot on the correct note name and get back to their spot before their competitor does. Whoever is first with the correct answer gets the point, and the first team to 20 points wins tickets! #themusicroomatmidway #musiceducation #musiced #musiceducationmatters #fun #elementarymusic"

While the music plays, they will pass the tater tot. When the music stops, I'll display a note on the board. The person who has the tot must run and put the tot on the correct note name and get back to their spot before their competitor does. Whoever is first with the correct answer gets the point, and the first team to 20 points wins tickets! #themusicroomatmidway #musiceducation #musiced #musiceducationmatters #fun #elementarymusic"

Comment: gurl_fromcali said "🆘CODE RED🆘WILL BE 🔫 FRIDAY 3/6/15 by @freethechi "#LOUISIANA #SHREVEPORT #URGENT! 🔶 #Facebook page of Humane Society of Northwest Louisiana: "3/01/15 ***URGENT***
These Chihuahuas will be euthanized on Friday, March 6, 2015 if they are not pulled by a rescue before then! There are 30 Chihuahuas, males and females and unknown heartworm status. They were seized from a breeder. Please share and tag rescues so we can get these babies out in time!!
*Available ONLY to 501c(3) Rescue Organizations by rules of Caddo Parish Animal Services and Mosquito Control, located at 1500 Monty Street Shreveport, LOUISIANA 71107. THIS Companions of Caddo Animal Services﻿ PAGE IS RUN BY VOLUNTEERS, not employees of the shelter.

3/3/15 UPDATE: 
On 2/27/15 Friday, Humane Society of Northwest Louisiana pulled 1

On 3/2/15 Monday,
-Ninna's Road to Rescue - Benton, Louisiana pulled 2
-Pet Savers of Shreveport pulled 6
-Louisiana Dog Rescue pulled 2
-Angel's Heart Puppy Rescue pulled 8
-Stop Animal Cruelty in Hot Spring County (Arkansas) pulled 6

On 3/3/15 Tuesday,
- Humane Society of Northwest Louisiana pulled an additional 2 (the mother & baby that originally were not allowed to be pulled by rescues)

If you are interested in fostering or adopting any of the dogs pictured, please contact one of the rescues listed above.
We are hearing there are ONLY 4 LEFT in need of 501c3 rescue organizations. 
The shelter has told us 10-12 dogs from this same group seized will go up for adoption later in the week. For adoptions, you have to go in person to the shelter. $50 cash fee. You can also call the Caddo Parish Animal Shelter at 318-226-6624. There's a chance some of the 10-12 selected for adoption may end up in "Rescue Only" too as they are pending vet examinations."" via @PhotoRepost_app @jojoandgilbert @dixie812 @they_matter"

3/3/15 UPDATE: 
On 2/27/15 Friday, Humane Society of Northwest Louisiana pulled 1

On 3/2/15 Monday,
-Ninna's Road to Rescue - Benton, Louisiana pulled 2
-Pet Savers of Shreveport pulled 6
-Louisiana Dog Rescue pulled 2
-Angel's Heart Puppy Rescue pulled 8
-Stop Animal Cruelty in Hot Spring County (Arkansas) pulled 6

On 3/3/15 Tuesday,
- Humane Society of Northwest Louisiana pulled an additional 2 (the mother & baby that originally were not allowed to be pulled by rescues)

If you are interested in fostering or adopting any of the dogs pictured, please contact one of the rescues listed above.
We are hearing there are ONLY 4 LEFT in need of 501c3 rescue organizations. 
The shelter has told us 10-12 dogs from this same group seized will go up for adoption later in the week. For adoptions, you have to go in person to the shelter. $50 cash fee. You can also call the Caddo Parish Animal Shelter at 318-226-6624. There's a chance some of the 10-12 selected for adoption may end up in "Rescue Only" too as they are pending vet examinations."" via @PhotoRepost_app @jojoandgilbert @dixie812 @they_matter"

-Draw one or more of any of my characters from the time crew (and, while they're not my characters, Jack Harkness and the Doctor are okay, too.)
-There will be 3 winners, and the prizes that each gets is listed above ↑
-The entries can be ponies, wolves, humans, etc. etc. I'm not asking for a specific species, I'm asking for tons of creativity and cool and original ideas. -Tag your entries to #skubatimecrewartcontest to enter. -You can enter more than one time.
-Ends: Friday, 3 April, 2015 (day we get out for spring break I believe?)
//
Thanks guys!"
